There was a wooden platform outside the RV, and there would be a circle of lights at night, which was soft and warm. What was surprising was that there were many nuts, raisins, etc. I couldn't wait to eat a few of them, and they were as sweet as honey. After entering, I found that there were actually 4 beds, one with a bunk bed, and the master bedroom was actually a 3-meter king-size bed. It was the first time I saw such a big bed, and I was definitely not worried about falling off. The whole RV was very clean, the bedding and towels were washed white and soft, the toiletries were of first-class quality, the air conditioning and hot water were very powerful, and the 3-meter king-size bed room could really see the stars at night. The next day when I checked out, I forgot a backpack and the front desk clerk contacted us warmly for safekeeping and handover. I commend you.
